| Section | Key Points |
|--------|------------|
| **What it is** | A terminal UI (TUI) and SDK that lets you chat with Claude, GPT4, Gemini, and local models (Ollama, LlamaCpp). |
| **Quick Start** | `pip install consoul`  set API key env var  `consoul` for the TUI or `consoul chat`/`ask` for CLI. |
| **SDK Usage** | `Consoul(tools=True)` gives programmatic access to file ops, code search, image analysis, and cost/token reporting. |
| **Features** |  Beautiful Rich TUI (Textual) with themes, history, attachments. <br> Multiprovider AI models. <br> Builtin AI tools: file editing, code search, image analysis, bash exec, web search, URL reading. <br> Safety controls: permission policies, approval workflows, audit logging. |
| **Documentation** | Full docs at <https://consoul.goatbytes.io> covering installation, configuration, TUI guide, tool docs, SDK tutorial. |
| **Configuration** | YAML (~/.consoul/config.yaml)  profiles, model provider/model, tools, conversation history. |
| **Security** | Permission policies (PARANOID, BALANCED, etc.), command validation, audit log (JSONL). |
| **Contributing & License** | MIT license; see CONTRIBUTING.md. |
| **Tech Stack** | Textual, LangChain, Anthropic, OpenAI, Google AI, Ollama, LlamaCpp. |
| **Getting Help** | Quick commands listed, e.g., `consoul --profile local` or `consoul chat "Add error handling to calculate_total in src/utils.py"`. |
